"""""yace gakinan yar karamadake amma sai iya magana,to tundadai nibanada dann saike kihaifamin' namasa  bayakada,nayimasa kallon sama dakasa nace.kajecan kanimi maihaifamaka amma banibakam"danni...dankeme?yasareni da ido nayi saurin sunkuyarda kaina kasa'yayi murmushi tareda shafa 茩ansa yace jekiyi barci amma kitabbata kinyi mafarkina yau.nace allah yasawaka nayi mafarkinka najuya nashige ciki.yayi karamar dariya tareda shafa gefen fuskarsa.tunranarda sukayi karo da ita tun lokacin ta gwari  zuciyarsa"yajuya cikeda nishadi..
Tundana kwanta idan narufe idona sainarika ganinsa da sautin muryarsa,naja tsaki haka narika narika juye da kyar barci yadaukeni"washegari"koda mukafito dan tafiya school, shima lokacin yafito "basma da ummee sukagaidashi,niko nakawar dakaina gefe,yakalli gefendanake saiyayi murmushi,yawuce parking lot"muko munasaye munajirar diraiba"yafito damotarsa yazo yasaya inda muke"yace ummee haryanzu idin baizobane?tace Eh wlhy baizoba,yace kushigo nasaukeku school in,dasauri ummee tace to mungode,tace kuzomuje.basma tabi bayanta niko ko kallon inda sukema banyiba,ganin inasaye yasa ummee komowa inda nake tariko hannuna.zomutafi mana ba'd'do zamuyi letti fa,nace kudai kuje nidai bazan shiga motarba,ummee tace haba RUMAINA sokkmu makara kinsan yaushe idi zaidawo daga inda yatafin,basma tace haba anty RUMAINA kizo mutafi mana...nacuno baki gaba nace wlhy badun gudun kada naje nasha bulalaba da ba'abunda zaisa nashiga motarna.basma tashiga gaba nida ummee muka shiga baya,yy wa motar key muka fita "yauma kamar kullum haka narufe fuskata harsaida  muka bargurin sojojinna.kafin nabude ido.
 Abakin get in makarantar yasaya su ummee sukafita namika hannuna naciro school bag ina dayashige kasan sit namika hannuna jikin murfin sainajita rufe,nadago kaina nasaci kallonsa sainaga niyake kalla tacikin mirro nayi hanzarin komawa tadayan gefen.harna zura kafata zanfita.yace dana sani dabandaukokiba nabari yau azanemin ke"nace saikasa azanenin ai"nafice abina,yadaga murya yace magananniya"nidai shigewa nayi batareda nakuma kulashiba"karfe 4 akatashemu" mukafito bakin get,tundaga can nahangi motar binsa nayi dakallo kamar nagane motar"harya iso yafaka agefenmu"ummee tayi murmushi tace 'ba'd'do allah yataimakemu,dahaka zamuyita sayuwa bamusan ranar zuwan idi'ba"ga Anas yazo zaimaidamu gida"kawarda kai nayi nayikamar banji abinda tafadaba"basma tace aikam,gashima yana magana kuzo muje"ummee tariko hannuna "najanye"tace kizo mutafi mana kinfasan idi bazuwa zaiyiba,kuma munabata masa lokacine"yanzuhaka daga gun ai kinsa yake yazo dan yamaidamu gida.nace bazan shishigaba"tace to jiran idin"zakiyi?nace Eh kuje xanzo daga baya"ina juyowa muka hada ido'dashi nayi saurin kawarda kaina.ummee tabudi baki zatakuma magana"saiga jiniyar sojoji" zasuwuce,ai dasauri nariko hannuta najanyota mukayi jikin motar.dasauri nashige cikin motar.ummee datasan abinda kefaruwa saitayi dari.tace mutum sai uban tsoro amma yace zaiyi kafiya"tunda nakafa kaina jikin sit bandagaba harsaida ya daidaita parking a parking lot kafin nadago kaina"
Nayi saurin fita daga motar banko jira basma ba nawuce abina"yakalli yadda nake sauri sai yy murmushi"inashiga natube uniform nafada bathroom"nayi wanka rareda dauro alaula.nazo nagabatar da sallah" ina'idarwa "naciro daya dagacikin kayanda baba yasayamin lokacin musabaqa damukayi"atamface rigada zani dinkin fisis" 
Bakaramin daukar jikina yy ba, simple mekeup nayi,sanna nafito parlor"asaye nasami mommy tana ganina tace "yauwa RUMAINA dama yanzu nakecewa basma takirawoki,to maza jeki dauko mayafinki mutafi shopping"nace to nakoma nadauko hijjab ina,koda nafito natar daharsun tafi gurin mota nayi saurin fita"sule driver mommy yaja"muka nufi jippato" shopping sosai mukayi"mommy tace nadauki duk abinda yamin,bawani kaya nadibaba"duk kayanda basba tagani saitace zaidace dani"saita saka cikin basket inda kerike ahanuna"haka tarika jida min kaya..muka fito bayan mommy tabiya,muka komo gida..
Sule driver yajudo kayan yakawo parlor,nadauki na mommy nakaimata bedroom inta,sanna nazo nadibi nawa nakai bedroom ina "nashirya kayakin cikin wardrobe "nashiga 
Bathroom nadauro alaula..bayan nayi sallah nadau wani dogon riga acikin shopping ina"nafito nanufi part insu ummee, 
Saiwaige waige nake"gani nake kamar zan yi karo da kare"saijinayi ance
Bakiganni bane kike dubani ko "to ganinan dan nasan ni kk tawaige"
Najuyo dasauri, nakallesa saikuma najuya" yy saurin shan gabana tareda nade hannusa akirjinsa,yace Eh mana ni kk dubawa dangashinan kintabbatarmin"nahade rai nace wayafada maka akanmekuma zan dubaka kayimin me"
Yace "akan zuciyarki takasa hakuri darashin ganina" "kamar yadda  nawa zuciyar takasa jurehakan"RUMAINA yakira sunana,ya ilahi,
yanayin yadda yakira ni saida yataba zuciyata, sainaji kamar shikadai ya iya kiran sunana dakyau"
yace tunranarda nafara saki a idona,nakamu da sonki da kaunarki"inafata kema kisoni' mugina sabuwar rayuwa mai kyau dasafta...zaikuma magana nayi saurin cewa.dan allah malam bani hanya nawuce.bamusu yakauce gefe "niko najuya madadin natafi inda zani saikawai nasinci kaina dakomawa inda nafito"
kodana shiga daki,nazube akan gado tareda rintsa idona"ranar banyi wani barcin kirkiba"washegari bayan nayi sallah sai asanna nasamu barci mai nauyi yadaukeni"kasancewar yau  Thursday ne,bani nafarkaba sai wajen   10 nayi mamakin barcin danayi"harkuma alokacin banbarjin abinda zuciyata takeba tunjiya"haka nalallaba nashiga bathroom nayi wanka nafito" nashirya cikin bakar doguwar riga acikin shopping inmu najiya" nafito parlor  nahaura dinning table" duk tulin kayan karyawa dake atare agun haka nakasacin komai sai tea kawai na iya sha"nakoma daki nadau rigar ummee natafi part insu"adaki natadda ummee kwance"nahaura kan bed in' tamike zaune tana fadin,ba'd'do,yadai naganki silent haka kobakyajin dadine?nace lfyta lau,namika mata laidar kayan.takarba tanacewa menene wanna nace kiduba kigani,tsarabarkice,taciro rigar tanadubawa tace gaskiya ngd wanna tsarabar tayi matukar yimin kyau"nidai kwanciya nayi inabinta dakallo yadda tasaka rigar yymata kyau"tacire rigar taninke ta aje gefe"tazauna kusa dani,tace RUMAINA mekedamunki?danni bahaka nasaba ganinkiba"shiru nayi banbata amsaba"takafeni da ido,RUMAINA har idan kindaukeni kawa aminiya kuma yar'uwa kamar yadda nadaukeki"to inaga dankinfadamin masalarki bawani abu bane,dannima nafada miki damuwata bawata masalabace danni nadaukeki yar uwata...natashi zaune nace ummee Anas ne..tace Anas to meyafaru dashidin?waicewa yy yanasona ummee bantaba jin wani yanayinda aduk sanda wani namiji yace yanasonaba,amma  tunda Anas yafurtamin wanna kalmar nakasa samun sukuni arayuwata"ummee inajin damuwa mai sanani azuciyata,nakasa fasra kalardamuwar danakeji araina"tace kema kina sonshine shiyasa kkjin wanna yanayin"nace nima bansaniba................

""""""Ummee tace,hakika Anas bayada wata ai bu,munyi shekara dashekaru dashi agidanna bantabagani kojin Anas ya ai kata wani mummunar abuba"kikarbi soyayyarshi dannasan itacema kedamunki azuciyarki"naja nummfashi tareda komawa nakwanta"ummee tarika bani baki harnaji  suciyata tadan samu nusuwa amma damuwakam nanan kamarjiya"nadanjima kadan adakin daga bisani nakoma part inmu"inashiga parlor natadda anty suraiya matar uncle ali" kanin mommy wadda sukeda zama acikin garinna unguwar fadamarmada"na isa inda take,nagaidata tareda daukar yarta ameera" dasakin fuska ta amsa gaisuwar,nan nazauna anata hira nidai murmushin karfin hali kadai nakeyi...muna nan zaune uncle ali yashigo,dasallama duka muka amsa masa sallamar"yasamu daya daga cikin jeren kujerunna yazauna"suka shiga gaisawa da mommy,basma tagaidashi.nima nagaidashi"ameera tunda taganshi tashi zillewa ahanuna,mommy tace ji yarna dan kinga dadynki shine zakirika zillewa"mommy tace dani mikata wa babanta"nadagota nazo namika masa ita"dama ala'ala nake nabar parlorn dan irin kallan dayakemin kullum idan yazo gidan shiyake kanmin yanzu"inajuyowa muka hada ido da anty suraiya sainaga tacanzafuska,nayi saurin barin parlor din"nashege bedroom"yau adaki nawuni nakasa gane abinda kedamuna"hargarin allah yawaye"

""""Nayi saurin rufe fuskata"cikeda jinkunya dan banyi zaton yana jinaba"yy murmushi tareda shigewa cikin mota,muma mukashiga yatada motar" duk yadda yaso muhada ido' firnaki kaina asunkuye har muka isa gida"yana daidaita parking  mukafita,nanne idona yy kokarin haduwa danashi namma nayisaurin kawar dakaina"najuya dasauri"nabar parking lot in,bin bayana yy cikeda shaukin so"
dadan guduna nashigo parlor da murmushi dau ke afuskata.ganin wanda ke zaune cikin palon yasani saida gudun danake"saida na iso sakiyar palon kafin nace inayini uncle ali"lfy lau yace idonsa akaina"nayi saurin barin parlor in danni banason kallonda uncle ali"yakemin inna"
Kodana shiga bedroom inatube uniform nafada bathroom nayiwanka tareda dauro alaula"bayan na idar dasalla"na bude wardrobe naciro doguwar riga pink wacce akabita da kwalliyar white in duwasu masu daukar ido"nasanya rigar ajikina"inajin wani irin shauki hadeda nishadi dukda damuwarda nakejinta acikin raina wacce nakasa fassara ta"duk sanda zuciyata zata fara tunano wannan damuwar sainayi kokarin danneta"kokari nake dazuciyata ta amince da son Anas"ce kehaddasamin hakan"

 Bayan nayi sallar isha inazaune akan sallaya ummee tashigo tazauna bakin gado"bayan nagama dukkanin addu o'i na namike na nade sallaya nacire hijjab"na ajesu ama'ajensu" ummee tace' ba'd'do"Anas nefa yadagoni dayanzu nakwanta barci"waisainazo nakira mishike"nace ayya (my  blood )kamar yasan nima tunaninsa nake"mujeko"

馃吙 19馃憠馃徎20




"""""nidai shiru nayi inatunani"taya zan gaskata abinda ummee tafadamin"bayan mutumin danagani adakin "mommy maisuffar larabawane,to taya zan yarda daba gamo nayiba"bayan ninaga aljanin balarabe da idona"
Kasa hakuri nayi"nace ummee toh...saikuma.nayi shuru"ummee tayi murmushi tace kibar tantama ko shakka" dazu dazan shigo nan naga motoci a parking lot"
Sanna naga  sojoji asama dakasan gidanna"ko shakka babu ya IB" ne yazo"munfashi nasauke wani bangere nazuciyata hankalina yakwanta da jin cewa ba gamo nayiba"wani bangaren kuma,dinbin tsorone najin cewa sojoji sun cika gidan"gashi shikansa mutumin danaganin sojone to inda yatashi ya harbenifa"nadafe kirjina cikeda tsoro"nace ummee to yanzu taya zamu tafi school nidai allah bazan iya fita nayi ido hudu dawadanna mutanenba"gaskiya saidai in yau bazani school inbakam"
Ido ummee taware"kina nufin yau bazaki school ba?to exam inkumafa?namma shiru nayi dan kaina gabadaya yagama kullewa"yadai zama dole naje school saboda muna exam"to amma taya zan iya fita daga gidanna bayan ga sojoji cike agidan"saikawai nafara hawaye harda shashaka,ummee tabude baki cikeda mamaki nata kallona"tace ba'd'do" menake gani haka,nitunda nake bantaba ganin matsoracin mutum irinkiba"to sai akace sojojin cinyeki zasuyi kkm harbinki zasuyi"nace allah ummee tsoronsu nakeji banason ganinsu"narasa yadda akayi haka kawai natashi nasinci kaina dajin tsoronsu"dukda nasan sudin mutanene amma saina rikayimusu kallon wasu daban"
Ni inaga karshen zamata yazo aginda danni bazan iya zama dasu tareba,
Haba RUMAINA"kada kisake fadan wanna kalmar har idan mommy taji "bazataji dadiba,akan wani dalilinki kice zaki bargidanna"to inamai tabbatar miki mommy ma bazata taba bari hakan tafaruba"dan itama irin daddy ce...saitayi shuru kamar meyen nazarinwani abu"saidaga bisani tace"allah sarki daddy allah yajikanka darahama"daddy mutumin kirkine"bazan taba mance alkhairinsa agaremuba,dukda kasancewar lokacin ina yarinya"nakalleta nace waye shi daddyn?
Tace "alhaji bashir nakowa"shine maiwannagidan"
Tun muna jahar plateau state "abbana suke taredashi"alhj bashir nakowa"lakabine damutane sukasamasa"shi nakowane" duk inda yazaga cikin kasarmu Nigeria"har kuwa kasashen waje"taimakonsa baya yankewa "baya banbance dan kasarsa da wanda bakasarsu dayaba""adalcinsa da taimakonsa"shiyasa ake kiransa da nakowa"
Duk shekara yakan zaga kauyuka harma dabirane"dan taimakon gajiyayyu da marasa galiyhu"yakan dibi mutane bila adadin"masu karfin cikinsu yabasu aikinyi acikin masana'antarsa"wadanda sukarigada sukajikkata"saiya killacesu"guri guda"yawadatasu da kayan more rayuwa" watarana yakaiwa garin shandam ziyara" duk unguwar dayashiga motocinda suke biyedashi"hakazaisa kowa yasauka haka zasu rikabin layilayi na unguwar dakafarsu"suna diban mutane"irin wadanda basada aikin yi inna dakuma matasa wadanda sukeson bata kansu daharkan banza wato shayeshaye"ahaka harsuka shiga unguwarmu"to anan suka tadda abbana"zaune akofar gida"har dashi acikin mutanen dasuka diba, koda  abba yazo yasanar wa umma abunda ketafiya umma tayi murna sosai nan mukafara shiri"washegari dasafe mota tazo tadibemu dayan kayakinmu bayan munyi sallama da yan'uwa""motar tadibemu
Saicikin garin bauchi" daddy yabamu gidansa dake unguwar federal lokos"yakuma  baiwa abbana manager nagidajen mansa dasuke cikin garin nan" kayakin abinci kuwa kanwani yakare za akawo mana wasu"akasani amakaranta "ya auwal shima yacigaba dakaratunsa anan" haka muka cigaba darayuwarmu cikeda kwanciyar hankali"
 bayan wasu shekaru"lokacin ya auwal yakammala karatunsa"damasuna soyayya da anty aisha"nan daddy dakansa yaje yanimamasa"aurenta"bayan auren ya auwal"dawata uku"abba yakwanta ciwo,satinsa daya ubangiya yakarbi ransa"munyi kuka kamar zamuyi yy"haka daddy yaji mutuwarsa sosai"bayan arba'in' din abba "daddy yazo yace mushirya gobe mota zaizo yadebemu mukoma sabon gidansa  dayakoma shima sati daya dayawuce alokacin"
Haka kuwa akayi "washegari muka dawo gidanna"aranar anty asma'u,damijinta malam suma suka dawo gidan"part guda daddy yabamu"muka zauna tareda su auny asma'u"
Sosai daddy kekula damu"hakama mommy"alokacinne akabaiwa Anas"masayin abba"ya auwal kuma mataimakinsa"
arzikin daddy  kuwa saidada bunkasa take"duk inda kazaga afadin kasarna ke harma da makotan kasarna"bawanda baisan alhaji bashir nakowa ba"kamfanoninsa gidajen mansa motocinsa kamadaga kananu har izuwa manyan tireloli"duk in dakikaga" ***I'B NAKOWA"
Tofa nasane"sunan ya ibrahim ne ajikin kowace kaddararsa"wato ***GENERAL IBRAHIM BASHIR NAKOWA"
ranar Monday daddy yy shirin tafiya abuja"ranar ikon allah saiyace bazashi a jirgiba"amota zaitafi"saida yabi kan mutanen gida danawaje kaf yy musu sallama"kafin drever yaja sukatafi"harsunkusa shiga abuja"motarsu tayi hasari"cikin gaggawa akakaisa asibiti " kankace me mommy tabi jirgi tatafi abuja"awa hudu dafaruwar hakan allah yakarbi rayuwarsa"dalabarin yariskemu"bamukadaiba hatta Nigeria saida  tagirgiza"dan kuwa anyi babban rashi....hankali yatashi sosai darashin daddy daga karshe aka fauwalawa allah komai"
Bayan rasuwar daddy da wata biyu,umma tasanar wa mommy da zamu koma garinmu"mommy tanuna bacin ranta sosai "tace dansaboda alhj yarasu shiyasa za afara gudunsu ko"umma tace bahaka bane"duk yanda umma taso fahimtar da mommy dalilin tafiyar mommy tace sam bazata taba fahimtaba"hakadai muka cigaba darayuwa agidanna"
Ummee tashare kwallar fuskarta" tace'  alkhairin familynna mai daurewane"dukda daddy yarasu amma ayyukan dayake na alkhairi yananan yana cigaba da numfashi adoron kasa"dan kuwa mommy da ya ***I'B "suncigaba daga inda daddy ya yasaya"
Tace RUMAINA mommy bazata taba barinki kitafiba dan haka kimadaina mafarkinna"
Nima nadan share kwallar idona dukda bansan daddy ba amma saida naji mutuwarsa yanzunna datake fadamin"nace allah yajikansa yasa aljannace makomarsa"tace ameen"
Tamike jiki bakwari tace tashi mutafi,kada mumakara"dakyar na iya mikewa saye,dan gabadaya jikina yagama sanyi"a palo muka tadda basma saye,muka fito kaina sunkuye nakan kame annun ummee,har saida muka shiga mota kafin nasaketa"nanma nakifa kaina asakan kanin cinyoyina har saida  muka isa school kafin nadago"
Koda akatashemu drever yazo yadibemu,addu'a narikayi araina allah yasa kada  mutadda sojojinna agida"yana daidaita parking muka fito ummee tafisge hannuta tagudu tanayimin dariya"dasauri namasa inda basma take nariko hannu ,nayi raurau da ido zanyi kuka tayi saurin c茅wa maiyafa anty RUMAINA?"nace basma sojoji sojoji'banason ganinsu"tace kai anty RUMAINA ina sojojin anan sudasuke can suna saron get mezai kawosu nan" idanma dazu dasafene kkgansu to saboda ya ***I'B jiyane yadawo to yazama dole sukwana acikin gidanna,kuma yau sunma tafi ragowar kuma suna can bakin get" sai yanzu naji hankalina Nace saura 6 Mon nacika 16 yeah"yace anya kuwa lissafinna daidai yake kuwa?naturo baki nace mekk nufi,yace hmm  bakomai"aransa yace dole mana yarinta natattare dake"afili kuma yace ashefa kingirma"todai soja basa kashe mutum haka siddan saida wani kwakwarar dalili"sukuma dakk ganinsuna,bakaramin taimakonmu sukeba dankuwa su suke saron kasarmu nigeria keharma da kasashen waje"nikaina wani lokaci nakanji sha awar zama soja dan nima nawaiwa kasata kariya"dasauri nace kai allah yasawake maka"aikuwa idan kazama soja ace alokacin munyi aure "idan zaka shigo gida saidai karika tube kayanka tundaga kofar gida"sanna kuma kacanza fuskarka daga kalar nasunna "yadawo yanda nasaba ganinka"barema bazaka zamo sojaba danni banaso" yace bakiso duk inda kk shiga arikacewa ga matar jarumin sojanna"nace  a'a nidai banaso"yace to shikena'yamikomin laidar dake hannusa "bin laidar nayi dakallo batareda nakarbaba"yace karba mana,namika hannu nakarba ina fadin menene wanna?yace wayace nasaimiki"nafiso kodayaushe narikajin muryarki"damurnata nashiga bude laidar,kai amma ngd sosai....."yace kidaina yimin godiya saboda bb ita asakaninmu"nayi murmushi cikin jin dadi na ce ammafa ka iya zaben waya gaskiya wayarna tayimin kyau..yace sosaima kuwa aini komaima na iya zabensa kikalli kankimana kigani"duk wanda yaganki yasan bakaramin jarumi baneni wajen iyazaben maikyau" uhm haka kacekam"yace hakannema,hira mukashigayi sosai harwajen 10 o'clock"kafin yarakoni bakin kofar palo kamar yadda kullum yasaba" koda nawaiga haryanzu yana zaune kamar dazu,nayi saurin kawarda kaina nashige ciki"

"""""""koda mukashiga parlourn gidan mai aikin gidan kawai mukatarar"basma tace tayiwa hajiyar magana,tace toh"mukasamu guri mukazauna munajirar fitowar mom insu nazeerat"can saigata tafito "mukagaidata ta'amsa cikin sakin fuska tana tanbayar ya h mommy take mukace lfyrta lau"namikamata Envelope,takarba taciro nata dubawa"karar takalmine yagauraye parlourn jikake kwaskwas ayangace takaroso tazauna kusada mom inta batareda takalli inda mukeba"tace laa mom yanzu dama zani gidan mommy kena danna karbo ashema ta aiko dashi din"tamiko hannu takarbi Envelope tazaro invetation card in masuyawa tamika mata sauran,tamike saye mom barinakaiwa friends ina"mom in tace to"tafita agidan,mom in nazeerat tadubemu tace bari na dauko muku tukuicinku tamike tashige ciki"tafito daukeda wata yar karamar jaka tamikawa basma "basma tace No mungode,kibarshi kawai,tace a'a ba ayi hakaba kukarba dan allah,kamar bazata karbaba saikuma tasa hannu takarba mukace mun gode"mukafito driver yamaidamu gida....
Kwana biyunna kewar gida nayawan damuna,inason naji muryar mama da baba"yaukam tunaninsu yafinakullom"namike jiki bakwari nafito parlour"mommy nazaune na isa nazauna.nayimata barka da rana"tadubeni cikin kulawa tace. RUMAINA meke damunki kobakida lfy ne?nagirgiza kai "lfyta lau "yanayinki yasauya kamar bakijin dadi kokintashi abarcine?Eh nace atakaice,mommy kokinajin labarin mama ko yasuke oho"yanayin danayi maganar yasa mommy yin yarkaramar dariya,saida nalankwasar dakaina nayi kalar sausayi kamar wata baby kafin nayi maganar"mommy tariko hannuna tajanyoni kusada ita,RUMAINA ai kinyi matukar kokari ace duk jimawarkinna baki taba jin muryar mahaifankiba"tadau wayarta dakegefe da ita talallasa saita danna call "bugu biyu aka daga kamar amafarki naji muryar mama tana sallama.mommy ta amsa matasallamar nan sukashiga gaisawa "bayan yan gaishe gaishe  kamar yanda manya sukeyi"mommy tadaura dafadin ga diyata zakugaisa,tun farkon jin muryan mama bakina yakasa rufuwa dan murna.nace ina yini mama "mama tace lfy lau RUMAINA yakaratu nace lfy lau alhmdllh"tace to madalla "mama baba yana gida 
ne?a a bayanan saidai idan yadawo saiyakira kugaisa,nayi saurin cewa mama zanma kiraki anjiman zankarbi numbern ki sainakiraki dawayata"aina kksamu wayan?shuru nayi tareda rufe fuskata"mama takuma cewa RUMAINA bamagana nakeyimikiba"komawa nayi nakifa fuskata acinyar mommy inadariya kasakasa"mommy tace ai bazata baki amsaba sirikinmune  yasaimata nima boyemun ake"shuru mama tayi saican tace a lallai shiyasa bazata  bada amsarba" mommy tace dama inasoma nazo dan muyi magana anshi Anas in wato yaron dasuke nima da ita RUMAINA"mama tace to shikena"tafada atakaice"nan sukayi sallama  mommy takashe kirar" daga bangaren mama koda mommy takashe komawa tayi tazauna tayi jugum tana tunane tunane azuciyarta"nidai bansan abinda take sakawaba"saidai jidanayi tace allah kafimu sanin abinda kefaruwa kazabarmana abinda yafi alkhairi...
Mommy tadago ni tana fadin to ai maman batanan koyau nima kunyar tawa akeji"uhm nikowayarma ba ataba nunaminba barena sanyamata albarka,nan madariyar nakumayi inarufe fuskata"tagirgiza kaitayi yaro kena tafada tareda mikewa tashiga bedroom"nayi saurin daukar wayanta naciro number damukayi wayi waya da mama"nashige bedroom,ina shiga nadanna kira"mama tadauka nayi mata sallama,tace RUMAINA kece? Nace Eh mama,sabuwar gaisawa mukakumayi"mama tace wai wanene yasaya miki wayar,saida narufe fuskata nace mama Anas ne"wanene kuma Anas?nace anan gidan yake,mama tace RUMAINA meyasa kika hada soyayya dakaratu"wayabaki damar yin soyayya dawani kada kisake babanki yaji wanna labarin"saikuma tasausauta muryarta daga fadan datakemin"takira sunana ahanki"tace duk abindaj kikaga  yasami bawa to dasanin ubangiji"kikasance mai hakuri dajuriya aduk inda kksamu kanki"nidai abazan fasa nanatamiba akan kirike mutuncinki kada kyalekyalen duniya yasa ki bararda darajarki tadiya mace"RUMAINA budurcinki shine yancinki agidanki na aure"mama tarikayimin nasiha mairasa jini"daga bisani mukayi sallama.....

__________________________________

Shirye shiryen biki saidada kankama yake, mommy dakanta taje Dubai tahado lefe...
Yausaura sati biyu daurin auren "tun lokacin ba'i sukafara zuwa sosai mommy take shirinbikin"kowani  gidan  TV dana radio idan kakunna saikaji ana zancen auren...
Abin mamaki kuma har lokacin ango baidawo Nigeria ba..ana saura kwana biyar daurin auren,nafito parlour natadda mommy dawaya akunnenta,nashigeta nashiga kitchen na aje plate indake hannuna"nafito sainaji tanafadin "yau inna nakeso kadawo wlhy kakiyaye bacin raina,nadai fadamaka kena"nan tasauke wayar akunneta...
Zanshige takirani,nazo indatake"tace kushirya yanzu zamufi "nace to,nashiga bedroom in basma nafada mata"kafin naje nadau hijjab ina....shopping mukatafi"bamu mukadawogidaba saidare"agajiye nashiga bedroom"natube kayanjikina nafada bathroom,nayi wanka tareda dauro alaula"nazo nagabatar dasallah"ina idarwa "ko ko muryar my nass ina "bansayajiba nahaye bed nandana barci yadaukeni"
Washegari "kodana nayi sallah barci nakuma komawa.banfarkaba saiwajen 11 wanka nafarayi nashirya cikin riga dazani na adamfa"nafito nanufi dinning nayi breakfats"ina gamawa nafita part insu umme nanufa dan tunshekaran jiya rabonmuhadu"can nahangota tanazuwa,saina saya najira takaraso,hararana tayi tace wato idan bannemekiba bazaki nimenibako"nace kai ummee yanzufa gunki zani ganin kina tahowane yasani sayuwa anan,uhm kamar dagaske nadauka Anas in yafara rabaki damutane tunyanzu"dariya nayi nace kai haba sharrikuma zakiyimishi nifa banason irin abunda kikeyi inna saikirikayiwa my nass ina sharri,tace sharri kogaskiya,dazu ai sukashigo shida ya auwal ,harwani dankiba   da haske yakara"nace dagaske indai hakaneko to gaskiya banji dadiba"au bakiso yy kiba da hasken kenan?No kibardai inasonta ita haskence banaso"tace kinafara kice bakison fari"inaso mana aini duk mace fara bakaramin kyau takeyiminba amma duk namiji fari allah ummee "bana sonsa kinsan allah intakaitamiki ma duk namiji fari inayimasa kallon dan iskane,akwai wani wanda yace yana sona dan garinmune sunansa sadam farineshi to duk lokacinda muka hadudashi allah banataba kulashi ke nikallonma dan iska nakeyimishi"amma mace fara tana mugun burgeni"shiyasa idan muka haduda nazeerat in ya***I'B bana gajiya dakallonta"ummee tace ammakuwa RUMAINA agaisheki wanna nazeerat in maikamada zabiyan itace takemiki kyau,kikalletafa kigani allah ni kyama takebani"farin nata yayi yawa,ai fari maikyau shine irin naki,itafa kadan yarage tazama zabiya"nace allah nidai inason farar mace dan tanamun kyau"namiji farikoma gaskiya baiyiba kinga shiyasa kullum bana gajiya da kallon my nass ina"tace lallaikam to dai kidaina yiwa duk namiji fari irin wanna fassara"dan gashi Anas nakin yafara komawa fari"...kinga namance umma tasani aikinefa bari naje sai anjima zamuhadu"nace to zanshigo nima...tatafi"najuya  zantafi sai karaf mukahada ido dashi nantake jikina yakama rawa nashiga uku yaukam nasan mutuwata tazo dan natabbata yaji duk abinda nafada..............

""""""bayabaya narikayi harna bace daganinsa"dagudu nashiga bedroom inasauke numfashi,nadafe kirjina allah dai yasa baiji abinda mukafadaba"koyaushenema yazo kasar oho sainatuna jiya naji mommy tana waya to komai akayi shitake bawa umurnin dawowanna"hmm,jin karar bude kofa yasani saurin dagokaina asorace,ganin basma ce yasani sauke numfashi ahankali"basma tace anty RUMAINA tundazu naketa nimanki kizomuje muwanke kanmu da lalle"bisy nifa bana samai akaina mama tahanani tace zaibatamin gashina"tace anty RUMAINA aidamake ba maiza asamikiba, idan kikasa mai akanki wazai iyakitsa kanki nima bangoyi bayan kibata sumarkiba"kawai gyaramikishi za ayi" nace to"taceto tashimuje"nace basai anjimaba,tace a'a anjimakuma yaushe zamusamu lokacin fita kawai mutafiyanxu"nayiwa ummee maga kitashi mutafi yanzukawai"namike nadau hijjab nasaka"mukafita"duk asorace nake kodamukazo kofa saida naleka kafin nafito"ummee ma lokacin tafito.wayata dake makale amarata tafara tsuwa arazane nacirota dan bakaramin razana nayiba ninagama mancewama da waya ajikina,damakuma asorace nake saigashi yadada soratani"ina duba maikinan sainaga my nass ne kekinan"nakara wayar akunnena"daga cikin wayan yace,ina zaku dannaga shirin fita kuke,nace unguwa zamu kana inane daharkaganmu nibangankaba"nafada inawaige"can nahangosa saye,najuyo nakallisu  ummee nace dan allah kudan jirani inazuwa,allah idan kk jima tafiya zamuyi cewar ummee,yanzuma zandawo,tunkan nakarasa inda yake mukesakawar junanmu murmushin kauna,harna isa inda yake,yakallene cikin kulawa yace inazuwa haka?nace gyaran gashizamu da lalle"ok to bari nadauki mota saina saukeku,nace to "nakoma inda su ummee suke,ummee tace hm dabakidawo yanzuba da muntafi,nace kutafimana ancemiki bansan hanyabane,kinsani amma kuma akwai dodanni abakin get.nace saime kosunananma wucewata zanyi,tace to basma zomutafi tazo daga baya.nace allah ba inda zaku"dariya sukayi "ummee tace nadauka kinfara zamowa jarumace.nace sosaima aini agun my nass ina namafi hakan,yacema zaikaimu saimudan jirashi...
Yazo damotar inda muke mukashiga"koda mukazo shiga saida ummee tayitamishi siya dan yace nashigo gaba su suzauna abaya"munatafe munahirarmu irinta masoya"harmuka isa yasaukemu yace zaidawo yamaida mugida idan mungama"mukashiga shagon, ma aikatangun sukabamugurin zama mukazauna"munsamu mutane agun. saida mukajira akagama musu kafin muma akafara yimana.andau lokaci maisawo kafin aka gama mana,duk wacce tashigo saitasaya takalleni watakamma bata iya hakuriba saida tazo tashafi gashina wacce aka nademun ita kamar gammo" bayabonkaiba duk nawa yafinasu kyau kamadaga gyarar gashi izuwa lallenda aka shinfidamin"itakanta wanda tayimin in saida abin yaburgeta har tanbayata tayi konice amaryar,nace a'a"saidaf magrib nakira my nass yazo yadaukemu,saisatar kallona yake"muna isagida, anakiran sallah...
Bayan nayi sallah " nafito parlour"ba'ine surcikin parlourn nawuce dakin mommy,dasallama nashiga dakin natadda mommy zaune abakin gado,tana ganina takama baki tace ina kukafito"nace mommy lallefa mukaje da gyaran gashi,bakiganiba.naja zanina sama harzuwa guiwa kafin nasake nacire dankwalena,garin cirewa nahada da ribom inda akadauremun gashina dashi,nan gashin yaware yazubo hargadon bayana yakuma rufemun fuskata,mommy tace ah lallaikam nagani yykyau sosai.natattaro gashin nahadesu nakuma daurewa.ina murmushin yabawarda mommy tayimin"tace RUMAINA je kitchen kihado coffee  kikawo,nace to nafita naje kitchen nahado coffee nadaura cop in kan dankaramin tray"nakomo dakin. nataddata tana waya'sainasaya batareda naje coffee inba tana sauke wayan, tace ah kaimasa mana kada yysanyi,tanunamin dahannu,nan wani kiran yakumashiga saitamike tafita"bin inda tanunan nayi da ido cikin rashin fahimtar abinda takenufi.kadan yarage nasaki tray inda kehannuna"yana zaune akan kujera yadaura kafafunsa saman table "fuskarsa babu ko alamar rahama. Sabar kidimewa kokarin aje trayn nake akara.saiwata  tunani yafadomin toma ai bayajin hausa.bakuma yanda zaiji abinda mukafada tunda dahausa mukayi maganar shikuma baji yakeba,nan nadan samikarfin guiwa"natako ahankali na aje cop in saman table gefen kafarsa,nayunkura zanmike"sainaji yace"ke!dagamin wanna abin anan yafada cikin sawa.....................

BANY NIYYAR YIN TYPING BAYAU AMMA SAIDA KKSANI YI"IDAN KINYI HAKAN DANKI CI ZARAFINANE TO KEDA ALLAH"SANNA KUMA KEBAKI ISA KISANI YIN ABINDA BANYI NINYABA KOMANI BANCE KIKARANTA NOVEL INA DOLEBA馃し鈥嶁檧BANSANKIBA BANKUMA TABA GANINKIBA"KEMAHAKA AMMA SHINE ZAKINIME KICI ZARAFINA"TOKISANI IDAN KKSAKE MAIMAITA ABINDA KKYI WLHY SAINASA ANNIMOMINKE DUK INDA KK"DAN NATABBATA SAKONA ZAI ISA GAREKI"





"""""""Zabura nayi wanda yysanadiyar barrarda coffee in"yamalale har zuwa kafarsa yajikamasa wando"innalillah,nafada dakarfi nayibaya cikin kidemewa"jikina narawa.sauko dakafafunsa yykasa yamike saye yanufoni  cikin bacinrai tareda zafin nama"baya narikayi harna bugu dajikin garu"ganin banada wata hanyar sira saina rufe ido na kam nadafe garun dahannayena biyu tabaya"hucinsa najidafdani nakuma kankame idona inagirgiza kaina"inazaman jiran harbe"munkai 5 mins ahaka batareda yacemin kalaba,sabar soro bakina yakasa furta kalmar hakuri"zuciyatako saibugawa take dakarfe, zuwa can sainadaina jin hucinnasa"ahankali nashiga bode idona.harnabude duka,sainaga bayanan nawaiga gefe dagefena ganin baya dakin gabadaya  "dagudu nafita adakin har inacin karo nakoma dakina nazube saman bed nakifa kaina nacusa fuskata cikin blanket"ahaka barci yadaukeni,bantashi farkawaba sai da akakira sallar asuba"bayan nayi sallah nakuma kwanciya,yaudai adaki nayini,su ummee da basma sunyi sunyi nafito firnaki sukatanbayi dalilin  rashin fitanan nace musu bakomai..alhalinko soronake kada nafita muhadu dashi.....
(Yau Sunday 17 November 2019) dubbannin al'umma sukashaida daurin auren  GENERAL IBRAHIM BASHIR NAKOWA da amaryarsa nazeerat alhj haruna"...
Zokuga murna wajen nazeerat" burinta yacika yauta mallaki ***I'B" aranarma fitowa tayi waizata gidan mommy"saida mom.nata tahata tacemata metake wa sauri haka bayanyau za akaita gidan"haka tahakura takoma daki badan tasoba"tarika kiransa awaya amma firyaki daukar kiran daga karshema saiya kashe wayar gabadaya"komawa tayi tajingina dajikin gado,tayi wurgi dawayan,wata kawarta sajida.tace haba nazee"meyasa kike damun kankine haka"yau wajen 4 days ago kktafaman kiransa baya dauka,tomeyekuma yanzukam ai yarigada yashigo hannu ko yaja aji ana" tofa idan akashiga dagaciki bafa zaija ajinba"dankuwa inamai tabbatar miki ***I'B nakowa" zaizamana atafin hannuki"dan nagama yarda da  gyaran hajiya suwaiba maida sohuwa yarinya"dan bantabajin ankushe gyararba"kedai kawai duk sanda yashigo hannu hmm"nazeerat takalli kawar tata tace,sajida kiduba kigani nadade ina birin duk randa namallaki ***I'B zan hada shagulgulan biki akalla kala goma"amma kiga kokwaya biyuma yaki yarda ayi  dana masamasama saicewa yy wainayi nikadai shibazuwa zaiyiba" reception inda za ajema yau saida naroki abokinsa sadiq yaje yasamesa hakanma dakyar yayarda"sajida tace,kedai kidaure daga yau ai yakare.duk sanda yadandani hadin suwaiba maida tsohuwa yarinya"saiya rainakansa,nazeerat tayi murmushin jin dadi"tace allah dai yakaimu daren gobe,nisaiganima nake goben yy min nisa nidama yau aka gamabikin akawase"sajida tace um saboda kwadayinki tamosa shine zakice haka"ina yanzu kikagama korafi anan"dariya sukayi sukatafa"tace mutumiyar kedai barikawai " ***I'B suffarsa yabaiyana afili bakaramin sugar zaiyiba"allah yakaimu goben kawai wani abun sai munhade dajuna....
Biki yayibiki yaucikingidanna babu masakasinke"narasa daga ta ina jama ar sukezuwa"yan jaridane takowani kusurwar gidan gamasu daukar video...."muna dakin anty asma'u can mukatare da yan makarantarmu dasukazo"
Yamma lis muka rakosu bakin get"nidai bankarasaba nayimusu sallama dan ganin gungun sojoji dake bakin get in farko"
Nakusa cikin jama arna harna isa parlour.jinayi anriko hannuna najuyo dasauri sainaga mommy ce,tace waiku bakwataba zama guri guda"tajanyoni cikin bedroom inta"tadauko wani jakka maidan girma tamikamin"karbi maza kuje kushirya,harda ummee nata naciki,nace toh"dakin anty asma'u nakoma,nan nataddasu basma, nacedasu gashi mommy tace mushirya dasauri,nafada inazuge zip din jakkar" nashiga ciro kayakin ciki,dinkakkun dogayen rigunane masu matukar kyangaske" iri dayane amma kowanne dakalarsa, saitakalma hadeda jakka"da gyale.da set in yankunnaye"kowani riga dakalar nasa, nan mukashiga bodewa kowa yadauki daidaishi" sanna mukayiwanka"mukayi salla kafin mukafara shiri" kowa yagama shiri saurani inanan inawaya da my nass ina" anty asma'u tafizge wayar tace kabarta sai anjima haka"takashe wayar "tace kalla kigani fa karfe 8 yanzu "har antafi reception mumunanan"watakilama har angu da amarya sun isa "zonayimiki mekeup dakaina dan muyi sauri"nandanan tashiga yimin kwalliya,ummee da basma sani sukayi agaba kowa tadaura hannu saman kumatu suna kallona"nace haba kadakucinyeni irin wanna kallohaka"anty asma'u tace kyalesu jekisa kaya kawai,cikin sauri nasaka kayan"anty asma'u tayimin dauri,my nass yakirani yace mudai harmun isa"saikunzo nace muma gamuzuwa.nakashe wayar.nadau hijjab inakokarin sawa.ummee tafizge"mekuma kkyihaka waikinanufin hijjab zakisaka?nace Eh mana,toda gyale kksonasa nifa bantaba sawaba"anty asma'u tace kisayau kawai kinji"nace allah ban iyaba"tace to kawo nasamiki "takarba tasamin ita akafadana"masha allah kamarkece amaryar,nakalli kaina amadube nikaina saida nayi hamdala ga ubangijin halitta...........

馃吙31馃憠馃徎32





""""""Tun bayan daurin auren ***I'B dayafita baikuma lekowa gidanba.nazeerat tayi kiran duniyarna wayarsa akashe"saita nimi sadiq tatanbayeshi kosuna tare"shima yace rabonsu dashi tunlokacin da aka daura auren" tace sadiq dan allah kataimakamin kadanaji kunya agun kawayena"kaga lokacinda aka sara natafiya reception inna yakusa yakamata ace zuwa yanzu munataredashi"dan allah kataimakeni sadiq,yace to karkidamu barinaje gidan nadubashi koyanacan"tace to ngd"takatse wayar,sadiq yashiga motarsa yanufi G.R.A yana isa gidan motar ***I'B nashiga yafito daga cikin motar yana kallon sadiq yasakai zaishige,dasauri sadiq ya'isoshi,yanafadin haba nakowa"kafasan lokacinda akasara natafiya gurinna,saurafa mintuna kadanne yarage"yakamata ace zuwa yanzu komai yakammala" dan allah kashirya yanzu danmuje gidansu nazeerat mudaukota" kada mubatawa mutane lokaci"tsaki yaja yajuya zaishige"sadiq yakumacewa dan allah kayiwa allah kashirya yanzu" mutane bazasuji dadiba zasuyi zaton angaiyacesune dan awulakantasu"pls ***I'B muje natayaka"shidai baicemasa kalaba yygaba sadiq yabibayansa"yanata rokonsa,dansanin halin abokinnasa"ba asashi kuma ba ahanashi idan yy niyyar abu tofa bbwanda ya isa yahanashi aiwatar da abun"ko mommy ma saitayi dagaske take iya tinkararsa dawani abun"yanada wani irin kwarjini  ne naban mmk"wanda inbakayi dagaskeba bazaka iya iya tinkararsaba"sanna baifiye son surutuba.maganakuma sada takeyi agaresa"dankuwa saika jima kanamasa magana inbaiyi ninyaba kotankawa bazaiyiba"saidai kagaji kayishiru.yana mugun son mahaifiyarsa Dan baya hada sonta dakomai.bayason bacin  rants kokadan...... yanashiga direct bedroom insa yashiga.sadiq yazauna a parlour yanacigaba da rokonsa"koda yashiga kayan jikinsa yashiga tubewa"ainahin kirar jikinsa yabaiyana"ya ilahi"allah yaworemasa kirar jiki namusamman"yadaura towel agugunsa,yashiga bathroom"yabata sawon lokuta kafin yafito"yanafita wani kamshi yagarwaye dakin,gaban Miro yaje yaja kujera yazauna,nan yashiga shafa mayuka masu sanyin kamshi,yataje gashin kansa yashafa masa mai.nantake gashin yashiga sheki da kyalle"yamike ya isa   gaban wardrobe yaciro"wani garnennen yadi,dakagansa kasan sai wane dawane nekadai zasu Iya saka irinsa,yasaka yadau hula irinsa yasa,yafeshe jikinsa da turaruka" sanna yasa takalmi yadibi wayoyinsa,yanufi kofa har ya isa kofa, saikuma yajuyo yakomo cikin dakin,ya isa gaban drw yabude yaciro wani katon files yabude yarika dudduba abubuwanda keciki,yadaura hannusa kanwani rubutu da akaja masa layi takasa.yaciro wayarsa daga aljuhu,yy copy in rubutun awayan"sanna yarufe yadaga zaimaidashi cikin drw  in saiwani Envelope  yafadi daga ciki ,yabi Envelope in dakallo ,saiya sunkuya yadauka,yarika juyashi ahannusa yana tunanin inda akayi yashigo cikin file in, yawurgashi cikin drw yarufe yamikesaye,komeyatuna saiyaku sunkuyawa yaciro Envelope in,ahankali yabude,nan wash hotuna sukabaiyana guda biyu,yacirosu dukabiyun yana karemusu kallo duka biyun mutun dayace aciki"yaware idonsa dakyau yanamaicigaba da kallon hoton,baya yarikayi harya isa  bakin gado har alokacin idonsa nakan hoton  ,dasauri yamike yaje yadau glass yasaka a idonsa ,dan  tantance gaskiyar abinda idonsa yanunamasa,tabbas gaskiya idonsa yanunamasa baimasa karyaba"saimai lura da fahimta zaigane sansanr damuwa dafirgicinda yashiga ayan mintunan na"kasancewar jarumin namijineshi, bakasafai ake iyagane damuwa ko firgici  ataredashiba .....
Jinshuru baifitoba yasa Sadiq shigowa dakin.haba ***I'B kaduba  agoga kagani mana,cewar Sadiq dasauri yamaida hoton cikin Envelope yabude wardrobe yacusashi cancikin karkashin kaya, yakulle yacire key in,yajuya yafita batareda yywa Sadiq maganaba,Sadiq yagirgiza kai yabi bayanshi....Sadiq shiyaja motar sukaje gidansu nazeerat,shidai yana zaune amma hankalinsa baya  gun gaba daya...har nazeerat sukafito dakawayenta,hartashiga cikin motar  tazauna kusadashi baisaniba ,tayitamasa magana baitankataba,harsaida tatabashi kafin yadawo cikin hayyacinsa"yajoyo yanakallonta,itakuwa ganin yana kallontan yasata yimasa kalamai tanawani kwantowa jikinsa"azahiri ita  yake  kallo abadini kuwa hankalinsa bayatare dashi,yynisan kiwo ......
 
Anty asma'u tace to kuzo mutafi,munafitowa"daidai lokacin motar ya***I'B" yakebarin gidan,nakalli ummee nace to yar rurutawa to inagashima shi angon saiyanzu zaitafi amma kinbi kin dami mutun yysauri yysauri,ummee tace todai nasan badani kkba kinayine da anty asma'u data hanaki waya da Anas,nace laa allah nibada anty asma'u nakeba dakenake,anty asma'u tace todai kuzo mutafi kubari idan mukadawo sai kuyi...mukashiga mota driver yakaimu"tundaga bakin get in hall in kakejin sautin kida, munashiga ciki kallo yadawo kanmu,nidai sai kakkame jikina nake saigani nake kamar bakaya ajikina"kasancewar bansaba sa gyaleba" nabi hall in da kallo,kai gurin yahadu ankawatashi da kyalekyale namusamman gurin tamkarrana"namaida dubana kan ango da amarya,sunyi matukar kyau sosai amarya nazeerat saiwage baki take"shiko angon ranna ahade tamau kamar kururci"wayata naciro daga cikin jaka. nadanna no in my nass ina,yanadagawa nace gamu mun iso kana ina"yace  kikalli gefenki,najuyo batareda nacire wayar akunniba,canna hangosa tadayan bangaren,najuyo inda su anty asma'u duke sainaga basanan"ashe harsun isa sunzauna"sunbarni nidaya saye"gashikuma gefenda sukazaunan bbgurin zama duk mutane suncike,hlm my nass yyminda hannu inzo"nakalli gefe dagefena kaf idon jama'a nakaina,dakyarna iya daga kafata nafara tafiya"ina zuwa sakiyar filin sai aka sauya waka,nantake jama arda kegurin suka kaureda tafi hadeda hele.sainaji kafata tadaure agun" nakasa koda mosawane"nan akarika tasowa sukazo sukarikayimin liki nayan 1k"nidai inasaye kamar fafeffeya"saiji nayi an rukoni tabaya"zanjuya sainaji hannu sakale akuguna,daf kunnena naji ance" Hii baby" arazane najuyo "  saiganin wani nayi saye dakagansa kaga dan tasha sailasar baki yake yanawani kanne ido" baya nayi dan mutane suncikegun bb wanda yalura da abunda kefaruwa... dasauri"***I'B"yamike saye daga inda sukezaune da amaryarsa" "nantake wutan gurin yadauke" nan guri yakacame dahayaniya,sojojin dake gewaye dagun sukashigo cikin filin,tareda kunna torch in wayoyinsu" hannuna akakuma rukowa nantake nafasa kara"jikina narawa,janyoni yy harbakin get batareda nagafuskar kowaneneba.saidai nasan komai akayi  wanna saurayinne" yabude mota yana kokarin turani ciki,nayi yunkurin kwace hannuna amma nakasa. Inaji inagani yaturani cikin motar yarufe,sanna yashiga yaje motar.ihu narikayi inabubbuga jikin marfin motar"gudu yake kamar zaitashi sama, bawani tafiya mainisa yyba yasaida motar"ga mmkna inakai hannuna jikin marfin sainaji yabudu,cikin sauri nafito daga cikin motar"sainanaganni agida , najuya gefe dagefena  gidane nan gida aka kawoni,najuyo dasauri jinkarar tadamotar kafin nayiwani aune har motar  tafita"dagudu nayi ciki inashiga nashige bedroom namaida kofa narufe tareda murda key ,nahaye gado nadunkule guriguda.jikina  nacirawa,soro maisanani yafufene,to wanene wanna,dazai taba jikina mekuma yasashi  maidoni gida"toko yy hakanne danyaji dadin aiwatar danufinsa akaina "nan nakumajin wani tsoron naJanyo blanket narufe kaina.....
Karfe dayana dare naji ana buga  kofa anakiran sunana muryar basma naji amma naki koda mosawa dan ganinake kamar kunnenane kawai yakemin karya,nadada dunkulewa..ahaka harbarci yadaukeni,
Washegari harwajen 11:am kofar narufe dukda inajin hayaniyar mutane amma nakasa zuwa nabude  kofar" Basma tazo tarika  buga  kofar tanafadin anty RUMAINA kibude mana mommy tanakiranki,namike naje tace  kai anty RUMAINA komu damukayi rawama jiya bamuyi irinwanna barcinba,takaraso ciki tazauna bakin  gado,tace      jiya mukarika nimanki bamugankiba,saida  mukadawo gida nagajakarki a parlour nace ashema kinrigamu dawowa,aijiya naji haushin daukewar wutanna harfa namike zanje nafara kwashe kudaden da aketayimiki liki saikawai wuta tadauke"hm  bakiga kyanda kkyiba afilin kamar  kece amaryar,nidai murmushi kawai nayi batareda nacemata komaiba dannasan Basma dasurutu, saikuma abunda  yafaru jiya yafadomin..katsemin tunani tayidafadin.ai jiya naji soron yadda ya***I'B yanaushi mutuminna kigafa naushi daya  yamasa yafadi kasa,kamar  yamutu"ashewai daukewar wutanna saboda kama mutuminne"bakiga sanda  sojojinna suka zo suka daukeshi Allah komosi bayayi,nayi dariyar  wata akusadani tashi tayi zatagudu saida  tayi MC yymaga akan jama a sukwantarda hankalinsu  mailaifine akakama kada suji soron komai kafin saita koma tazauna...mailaifi? nafada araina,race Eh mutumin jiyannan da ya***I'B yanaushesana kebakiji ance mailaifi bane,lokacinda wutarnan yadauke ai alokacin ya***I'B yakamashi,dasauri nakalleta danbanyi zaton maganar tafitoba................

"""""""Nakalli Basma daga  indanake saye Dan son kawarda maganar  nace   bakince mommy nakiranaba,tamike dasauri tace laa  kinga  namance kumafa tace  nayisauri dan  aikenmu zatayi" zomuje taruko hannuna mukafita,adaki mukatadda mommy.,mommy tace  saiyanzu akatashi abarcin?nayi murmushi tareda gaidata, tace kudauwanna kukaiwa nazeerat kuje driver yakaiku yanzu,tanuna jaka dake  gabanta,mukace toh nakaihannu nadauka mukafita. dama  da hijjab ajikina"darect mukafita.nakalli Basma nace  yanzu gidan gidansu can zamukena,tace  a a bajiya ankawota gidan ya***I'B ba ,a unguwanna gidan yake banisa, nace OK muna saye  munajiran fitowar driver"ya***I'B yashigo da mota bayan yadaidaita parking yafito yasaya jikin motar dawaya akunnensa,yakalli gefenda muke  saiya kira Basma da hannu.tacedani inazu,nace to.taje  inda  yake,magana yy mata daga indanakedai banajin abinda yakefada,amma yanayin yadda yakemaganar zakafahimci dafada yakeyinsa,tadawo  inda  nake  tace kawo jakar namikamata tajuyadasauri taje    tamikamasa jakar" saitajuyo tazo tace zomukoma,munashiga parlour nasaya nace Basma meyasa kk kaimasa bayan mommy ce  ta aikemu,tace. cewa yy waimukoma zaibaiwa driver yakaimata bakiji masifar dayytaminba dama nima  basonzuwa gidan nakeba,

""""""" Nasakai nashiga harlokacin yana inda  yake sayen"inazuwa dafdashi wayata tashiga  ring, nadan gotashi kadan sanin  konagaidashi ba amsawa zaiyiba,sainadau wayar"nakara akunnena inafadin,my nass  bakatafi masallacinba?"yace  inahanyarzuwa kena. muryarki,nace muryata tayime? ikan girki kalakala"kula maidauke da tuwan danyen shinkafa da miyar shuwaka nayi serveng"dan tunawa da mama tanason miyar shuwaka,soyayyarsu da shuwaka haryasata dasashi acikin gidanmu"tunbana iya ci tayimimkarya. tofa warin  sigari nakeji,juyowa nayi inda  nafijin warin  kefita,saina  sincikaina dabin  hanyar "ahankali narika  kusawa cikin Flaw's" tarinarikaji dasauri nakuma kusa kaina"durkushe nagansa fuskarsa nakallon tacan, yadafe kirjinsa da hannu daya  yana tari .daya  hannun kuma rike  da sigari" ido naware  danganin halinda yakeciki,wa'iyazubillah"sigari yakesha"sainajuya dasauri tareda toshe  hancina,nadaga kafata zantafi sainaji naharde da wata flw "saijina nayi tim  akasa" sabar soro yasani mikewa batareda naji zafin faduwarba"dasauri yawaigo karaf mukahada ido"idanunsa ce  yagama cikani" yanzu dama  nashan  sigari"kai wa'iyazubillah....
Yau  Monday tun  a school nakejin jikina bayamin  dadi,kamarwasa saidada karuwa yake"harcikin kashina nakejin zazzabin nagasani"bayan antasomu kukadawo gida,haka nakwana da zazzabinna"washegarikam ban iya  tafiya makarantaba"  mommy tabani maganin zazzabi waikodun zazzabin zaisauka amma ina "dukda inacikin blanket amma banfasa rawan sanyiba" ganin yanayin jikinnawa yasa mommy kiaran family Dr"awaya"yashaida mata gashinan zuwa yanxunna"tace tashi kijekidan wasa ruwa dankidanji karfinjikinki kafin ya'iso"nace to,tataimakamim nashiga bathroom "adaddafe nayi wankan nafito" kodanafita sainatadda bata  dakin"dakyar na iya  isa  gaban wardrobe ,naciro doguwarriga mara  nauyi  nasaka,nakoma bakin  gado nazauna"nan wayata tabada haske saiku tadauke alamun yankewar kira"kasancewar wayan tana  silent ne" nadau wayar naduba sainaga missed call in my nass  yacika wayar "inakokarin binkiran saigashi yakuma  kiran'inadagawa  yace"  RUMAINA yajikinnaki" yanzu inayakeyimiki ciwo" kinci abinci kuwa kinkumasha magani???"gani zuwa barinazo mutafi asibiti"yanzunna"nayi murmushin  karfinhali nace,dasaukifa my nass  nasha magani kuma mommy ma takira Dr yace  yanxu zaixo yadubani"yace  Eh kodahakama sainazo naga yanayin jikinna naki  " Kadaibari lokacin dawowarka tayi,danjikin dasauki  bafayanda kknufin bane"yace  anyakuwa?tace dagaske nake,yace  toshikena,yace  kikula dakanki"nace kaima  haka"nakashe wayar"nan mommy tashigo  tace tosomuje ga Dr yazu,namike dakyar muka nufi parlour"nazauna tareda gaida  Dr"yace  lfy lau  yakin?nace dasauki" yace mekedamunki?nace zazzabine"yace  bayan zazzaba sai  inayakemiki ciwo? nace bb shikena"yace  OK,yadanmaso kusadani"yadaura bayan hannusa agefen wuyana"OH "sannuko" kaikawai nagyada masa, yace gyara barinadau jininki sainakai lab ayi  test,nace to,nagyara yaja  jinina "yacewa mommy hajiya  barinaje daga gun sainazo matada magani" mommy tace to badamuwa"yafita,nagyara kwanciyata aka asaman kujera,nan barci yadaukeni...maganar danaji akusadani yasani farkawa,sainaga mommy ce  da Dr,sai  Ummee dake  zaune kusada kaina,Basma nagefe"da rukayya harda goggo larai "Dr yace Hajiya ga result in test in da akayimata" saiyabude takardan ,yace ciwonta baya  bukatar magani " saidai abata nazafin jikinna saboda gudun illatasu"cikin rashin fahimta mommy takallesa ciwon bayabukatar maganikuma kamarya?yace inanufin tana  dauke dajunabiyu" arazane namike saune,banikadaiba hatta wadanda sukecikin parlour in saida suka dago amatukar razane.............

馃吙37馃憠馃徎38




""""""Nantake  nanimi zazzabinda nakejinna narasa, Innalillahi'wa'inna'ilaihirraji'un"shikadai nake  nanatawa, tun  inayinta acikin zuciyata harnazo inayinta afili"nantake hawaye yafara wankemin fuska,karankataf hankalin wadanda suke  parlour yadawo kaina" mommy takalli Dr tace am anya kuwa result inna namuce ko anyi   mistekne kakabamu nawasu" yy murmushi  yace haba hjy idan hakantafaru to yananufin munawasa da aikinmu kena"wanna shine result inta"hjy,wanna itace result in"Allah shikyauta yafada tareda mikewa saye,yywa mommy sallama yatafi"Rukayya tawaro ido tadaura hannu akirji,tace ciki,ciki gidanna'asamu irinhaka"aisai arikayiwa family nan wani irinkallo"dan duk kwatancen daza ayi dole sai ansa  da family nan tunda acikingidanna kk"ammadai gaskiya za abar abunfada"takumayimin wani kallo"saita mike tabar parlour"tana shiga daki'dawani irin salle da murna tazube saman gado tadau wayarta tadanna wani number takara akunnenta tanawani irin dariya..jimkadan takuma fitowa"tajuya takalleni sama dakasa"ta girgiza kai"dafadin lallaiwanna abu ai abunkunyace acikin gidanna saitakuma fita  daga  cikin parlour tayiwaje gaba daya..."mommy tarika  juya  takardan ahannuta,saikumata   kalleni saita girgiza kai" jinayi nummfashine yana sarkewa"saikokarin janyosa nake  dakarfi"goggo  larai tace keko yarna wanga batu gaskiyace" ido kawai nakura mata"sonake natan  tance shin idona  biyune koharyanzu barcin nake"ganin yadda nakeyi da ido yasa ummee  riko hannuna"niko  narike hannu natagam"mommy tamike saye tace ummee  taimakamata"taje  daki"tace toh,tajanyoni mukamike,har alokacin bakina yakasa furta komai saihawayi dazufardaketa ketomin"munashiga dakin,ummee  tazaunardani bakingado,tace RUMAINA shiru ban amsataba, takuma kirana nanma shiru nayi sai idona  danaketa warewa"tagirgizani "dakarfi,tanafadin RUMAINA ki amsamin mana kiyi maga  RUMAINA fadamin waishin gaskeyane abinda Dr yafada" sai  alokacin natabbata bafa mafarki nakeba,nariko hannuta dakarfi tareda fashewa dawani irin  kuka maisuma rai,yinake bbko kakkautawa"itama kukan tafashe dashi,tarungumeni mukarika caskar kuka,cikinmu bamairarrashin wani"saida  mukagaji dankanmu ,mukayishiru"sai  ajiyar zuciyarda muketa saukewa"harkuma lokacin hawaye baidaina zuba a idonaba" ummee takalleni takaihannnu fuskana tasharemin hawayen,saitace bad'd'o kibarkukanna haka'kinji kwanta kiyi barci"kai nagyada kamar  baby nagyara nakwanta"itakuma tamike tafita"inaganin Kiran my nass  sai  janyo wayarnayi nakasheta gabadaya"narufe ido dakarfi waikodun zandainajin zafinda zuciyata takemin...
Bayan mommy tashiga daki tajima zaune tana  tunanin wanna al'amarin,sainanata maganar  take acikin ranta "waiciki RUMAINA ce da ciki,hankalin  mommy yakai makurar tashi" takasa zaune takasa saye, bayankwana uku"
Nashafe wanna kwanakin cur adaki ,kodaidaida parlour bana  zuwa,kankace me kafgidan yadauka kowa yasan inada ciki,abinci kuwa mommy kesawa akawomin,basma takan shigo tazauna shiru dukda surutun tanna amma haka zata zauna tayi tagumi kusadani zuwa cankuma tafita"Rukayya kuwa kullum saitashigo dakin takaracimin hausa  da habaici tafice".. Bayan na'idarda sallar azahar,inazaune akan sallayar narafka uban  tagumi,basma  tashigo.tace mommy nakirana"saida naji gaban kirjina ya  yanke,dakyarna iya  mikewa inaji kamar  iska zai daukeni,a parlour nasami mommy saye da makullen mota rike ahannuta" tana  ganina tacedani kibiyoni"nabibayanta har parking lot"dasauri direba yadunfaromu tadaga masa  hannu alamar yada kata,tacedani shigamuje"nashiga nazauna  tatada motar  mukabar gidan" tafiya  maidan nisa mukayi sanna mukashiga cikin wani hospital da akarubuta,(city specialists clinic)munazuwa batareda bata  lokaciba aka shigarda mu  wani office鈥漡aisuwar sani  mommy sukashigayi da Dr din,Dr yace lfy hjy naganku da wanna ranar?lfy Dr yarinyace nakawo batajin dadi,yaceto  meke damunta"saida  tadanyi jim kafin tace,sonake ayimata  test,din ciki,juyowa yy yakalleni  dakyau sanna yace Ok.yaja jinina,sanna  yy rubutu atakarda, yakira wani nurse yamikamasa takardan hadeda jinin da yaja   "jimkadan nurse din,yadawo office in yamikawa Dr takardan,yafita" yabude takardan yakura masa  ido,saiyadago yakalli mommy "yace toh ciki dai akwaishi saidai karamine,danbaiwuci nasatikaiba" zunbur mommy tamike saye,niko numfashina kokarin fita yake ina  janyoshi"Dr yace lfy hjy bamatan aure  bace bako dannagadai tayi yarinya dayawa"murmushin yake mommy tayi,tace a'a bakomai mungode taciro  kudi ajakarta ta aje akan table,taruko hannuna muka fito"damugun gudu mommy tafigi motar  mukabar asibitin,kuka narikayi harmuka iso  gida namma takuma ruko hannuna harcikin bedroom inta,kafin tasakemin hannu "tacire mayafin dake  kanta tarika  fifita dashi dukdako sanyin  AC dake cikin dakin"tace RUMAINA wayamiki ciki,wayamiki ciki,RUMAINA wayamiki ciki!tamaso kusadani tariko  kafadata,tace fadamin RUMAINA Anas  neku" kifadamin mana!tafada  dakarfi,shiyamiki fade idanma wanine yamike feden kifadamin"cak  nayanke kukan. narika  jadabaya ina girgiza kai,mommy ba Anas  bane mommy bashibane,sainafashe dakuka,inacigaba dafadin wlhy bashibane.tace to waye idan ba Anas ba"kaikawai naketa girgizawa kuka yarigada yaci karfina,dagudu nafita adakin nakoma dakina nazube saman gado inawani irinkuka maicikeda bantausayi"ummee  tashigo  tasameni"tarikoni namike zaune, narirrike hannayenta,nace ummee waikam mekefaruwa daninekam,ummee  waidagaske ciki nakedashi gashi wani Dr yafada" meyasa mommy kezargin Anas  bayan ko amafarki nasan bazai ai kata hakanba"ummee  tace kibarfadan haka ,kedai kibarnamiji kawai,dannima nafara zargin sa"nace ummee my nass  din? tace kwarai,shikadaine saurayinki aduk fadin  garinna taya baza azargesaba"haba ummee  ,wlhy natabbata sonda Anas yakemin  bazaibarshi yaci amanataba"Anas son aure  yakeyimin bana  fasikanciba, ummee bazan mance ranarda Anas  yakefadamin  bayaso murika  kallon idon  juna saboda gudon fadawa halaka nayarda dashi bazai cutar daniba.hmm namijinko............

馃吙39馃憠馃徎40




""""""Ummee tace kibarnamiji kawai yawuci tunaninki" nidai nima  nafara zarginsa .idankuma  bashi din bane towanene?"cikin shashekar kuka nace ummee nima  bansani,abinda nasane shine  babuwani namijinda nataba kebewa dashi,kumani ba fede  akaminba'tace to mehakan kenufi"dole zaitabbata fede  akayimiki dankuwa ba'ataba daukar ciki batareda namiji da mace sunsadu dajunansuba,bad'd'o fede akayimiki"tayuwu wanda  yyhakan yy amfani dawani sinadari wajen gusarmiki da hankali  haryacimma burinsa"shirunayi batareda nakumacemata komaiba"tamike saye tace kikunna wayarki Dan Ana's nadamina dayawa,barinaje nadawo tafita" namike dakyar nashiga bathroom nayi alaula nafito nayi sallar la'asar,nadau wayata nakunna"kamar  jira  yake saiga  kiransa yashigo,nadau kirar tareda karawa akunne"shiru nayi batareda nace komaiba,RUMAINA yakira sunana nanma shurun nakumayi"yakumacewa RUMAINA meyake faruwanekam" wani irin  magana nakeji agidannane?saikawai nafasheda kuka"har ina  shesheka,cikin kukan nace my nass bansaniba"nibansaniba"bansankomaiba"kuka yacikarfina,nayarda wayan,nazame kan sallayar nakifu daciki,inawani  irin kuka..
Sauke  wayar yy yanabinsa da ido,subhanallah waishin wanna wace irin  lamarice"karar wayarce yadawo dashi daga  tunanin da yake"yana dubawa saiyaga mommy ce  kekiran,nasan za'yi hakan"yafada afili"cikin hanxari yanufi part in mommy"yashiga  parlour bb kowa saiya zauna asaman kujera,yana zama tanafitowa daga  bedroom,ta isa tazauna"yy hanzarin gaidata"ta amsada lfy lau" tagyara zama tace, Anas menene sakaninka da RUMAINA bayan alakar soyayya dakesakaninku wacce narigada nasane tuntuni' yace banfahimci abinda kknufiba"inanufin RUMAINA tanada ciki,kuma kasandai batada wani saurayi bayankai"dasauri yace subhanallah "wlhy mommy bayan alakar soyayya da  yarjejeniyar aure  bb wani alaka sakaninmu dayawuce wanna"zaki iyakiran ita RUMAINA gani gata zankuma maimaita abinda nafada yanzu" wlhy ni ba'irin sonda nakeyiwa RUMAINA bakena,shiru mommy tayi saikuma tace tashikaje zansauwala bincike akan lamarin" yamike  jiki bakwari yafita.dakinsa yashiga yazauna  tareda dafa kansa,dake  mugun saramasa, yadau waya daddanna tareda karawa akunne..inakwance akan sallayar har lokacin,sainaji wayata nakara dakyar na iyamike hannu najanyota"batareda naduba maikirarba,nadaga inakai wayar kunne naji muryar my nass  yanafadin,
Bayanni natabbata bakidawani saurayi"RUMAINA keshaidace tunda mukedake ko hannuki bantaba rikewaba"RUMAINA waye wanna wayeshi,kifadamin"meyasa kkyishiru tunlokacinda abinyafaru bakifadaba"meyasa xa ayimiki fyede kiyishuru bakifadaba???kiyimagana mana RUMAINA!yafada cikin karaji"bari jikena yakamayi,bakinarawa"nace wlhy bansaniba babu wani wanda  yymin fyeda"nibansan komaiba"bansaniba bansaniba wlhy bansankomaiba"nakarashe maganar cikin azaba dakunar rai,nakuma fashewa dawani irin masanancin kuka "yanda numfashina yafara sarkewa yasani sauke  wayar, nakuma kifuwa nacigaba dakuka wacce yanzu yazamemin abinci...
Yanajin sautin kukan akunnesa kasancewa  wayar baiyankeba,karar bude kofa yaji wanda  yasashi kallon kofar danganin maishigowar"gamamakinsa saiganin Rukayya yy" kallo daya yymata yadauke kai,danganin kalar kayanda kejikinta"bawasu masu mituncibane"duk sunbi sundameta duk surar  jikinta afili takowa tayi,ta iso  inda  yake,saiwani karkada kugu take.tazauna akujerardake (Fessing)insa tayiwani smile tareda kashe masa  ido,tace haba Anas yazaka zauna karika  tasarwa dakanka hankali  akan wani dankaramin abu"dankallonta yy danfahimtar inda  maganar  tata tadosa"tacigaba,kazo mugina rayuwa namusamman kamance da wanna yarinyar kaikanka yanzu zaka  gane  itaba sararkabace"inbanda sabar cin amana  irinnata tasallakeka takaiwa wani kato kanta haryabata ciki" idanma sotake tahole taji dadi,tahuta sosai"harta sallake kanka tajegurin wani kato  yanarkamata ciki"idan banda wauta irinnata yaushe zatasake harciki  yashigamata,batasan yadda tayiba"Anasa,kamance yarinyarna kazomugina sabuwarrayuwa"idanma kanada  wasu  yanbukatune duk zan iya  daukemakasu"tunda harta Iya cin amanarka tanadawani agefe tanajin dadinta kaitabarka,tunda tafara magana yakafeta da ido har takai  aya"wani irin  kallo yamata sanna yace idan nafahimceki"kinanufin kice RUMAINA binmaza take"tace sosaima kuwa nikaina shaidace,ita  tasan nataba kamasu dawani"kai kananan anacin amanarka kadauki duk yardanka kamallaka mata bakasan kalar holewar datakeba"nasan idan nafadamaka tunfarko bayarda  zakayiba"amma kaga yanzu ga gaskiya tabayyana"k....batakaiga kareshi maganarba tajisaukar lafiyayyeyar mari afuskarta"yakuma kaimata wani marin saitayi saurin  kaucewa"asorace take kallonsa hannunta akan fuskartaa tana  goga inda   yamaretan"cikin sananin bacin rai yanunata dahannu,yace, ke kinsan masayin wacce kkmuzantawa da aibantawa agareni kuwa"ke harkinada bakin cewa wata yar  iska"RUMAINA tawa kkyimata kazafi"to barikiji,koda  mata sunkare aduniya bazan taba saurarankiba,koda   ace abinda ake  zargi akanta ta aikatashi,toni  inasonta ahakan"banza mara  mutunci keharkinada bakin aibata RUMAINA"tafiki komai da komai" fitamin  adaki!!yafada cikin sawa.jiki nabari ta isakofa,saitaja tasaya takalleshi,tace.wlhy saikayi danasanin marin  dakamin wlhy sainajefa ta cikin fitina datashin hankali wanda yafi wanda takeciki yanzu"kumazakaga abinda zaifaru"yace saidai naga alkhairi,sharrikuwa saidai yadauwama akanki"tajuya fuuu tafita....
Washegari..
11:am
Dakyar nalallaba naje nayiwanka,inafitowa natadda anty Asma'u da ummee zaune abakin gado"na isa nazauna inda  suke batareda nace kalaba "anty Asma'u tace RUMAINA najuyo nakalleta saikuma nafashe da kuka" tace haba kekuwa kirage kukanna  hakamana  abinda yahanamu zuwakenan tuntuni nida Aisha saboda munsan dole zakiyi kukanna"kullon saina  tanbayi ummee tacemin kwana kuka kk"RUMAINA hakuri zakiyi darayuwa"wanna itace kaddararki"danke musulmace to yazama dole kiyarda da kaddara maikyau ko marakyau" takamo hannuna tace kiyi hakuri kinji RUMAINA in Allah yayarda Allah zaitona asirin duk wanda ya aikatamiki hakan"kidaure kirage  kukan dan  gudun kada yacutar da abinda ke cikinki,danshi  bashida laifin komai baimasan mai akecikiba kinjiko"nagyada kai alamar toh"tace yauwa" tashiga sharemin hawaye"sunjima sosai adakin sunata janada hira harsaida akakira sallar azahar kafin suka tafi..
Lokaci zuwa lokaci  sukanzo suyita jana  dahira"mommy ma kullum saita lekoni,yanzu batacika zama agidaba kasancewar shekara tazagayo tanazuwa garurruwa dan bada zakka abisa umurnin mijinta...kodana tashiyau hayaniya nakeji sosai acikingidan..............

馃吙41馃憠馃徎42




""""" Koda nakasa kunne sainaji muryoyin mutane dadama"cikikuwa harda  masu jajantawa mommy akan abunda yafaru,kowa nafadin albarkacin bakinsa.wasukamma cewasuke watakiladama halinane hakantuntuni yanzunedai asirina yatonu...,ummee tashigo tasameni zaune kamar  kullun, ta isa tazauna,inaganinta na kwakulo murmushi"kaikawai tagirgiza,tace bad'd'o yau  kinkwana kuka "nayisaurin cewa a'a"tace Eh mana baga idonki Yakunburaba" nace kainake ciwo shiyasa kkga idon yakunbura" tace uhm to sannu,tafadane kawai badon  tayarda da abinda nafadaba"muna hakankuwa saiga hawaye nafin gefen fuskata batareda nasan yanazubowanba,ummee tace toyanzukuma wanna menene?tanuna gefen suskata,nayisaurin kaihannuna fuskata  sainaji hawaye,haba RUMAINA kinaso kisawa kanki  ciwon zuciya,kiduba kkgani kekanki bakimasan hawayen nasaukaba"nayisaurin riko hannuta nace,ummee kukandanakeyi acikin zuciyatace tafito"narinsa ido,ummee bansan dawani ido zankalli mama ba.kullun maganarta baiwuce narike darajata kimata mutuncina budurcina shine yancina agidan aurena ba":ummee bansan yanda zanyi ba har idan mama taji wanna kazamin labarin"ummee natabbata kasheni zasuyi itada baba,saikawai nafashe da masanancin kuka.tace kiyishiru RUMAINA insha Allah zasu fahimceki,tunda badason ranki  hakan tafaruba" hakatarika bani baki tana  karfafamin guiwa harnadan samu sassaucin abinda nakeji azuciyata....haka rayuwa tacigaba datafiya.nidai yanzu rayuwata adaki takare dan  ko  school ba nazuwa ummee tayitayi firnaki hakatahakura tabarni, wayatama kashe ta nayi gabadaya najefata cikin wardrobe,____________yaukimanin wata biyu kenan dafaruwan haka, duk nagama fita haiyacina narame sai uban  haske danakarayi saikuma sawo dana  karashima kasancewar narame.....inazaune bisakan sallaya inatilawar ALQUR'AN" Basma tashigo tace hajja umma nakirana,hajja umma mahaifiyar mommy ce jiya tazo garin,kodana fito sandana saya  akofar parlour inatunanin yadda zan iya  shiga cikin jama'ardanakejin muryoyinsu,ba Iya yancikingidanna bane harda matar uncle Ali "damatar ya***I'B" sauranma ban Iya shaida muryoyinsuba,nasinkayo muryar mommy tanafadin,bansan taya zanfara tunkarar mahaifan yarinyarna damaganarnanba"hargarinsu naje amma nakasa zuwa gidansu,saboda bansan abinda zancemusuba idan suka tanbayeni lfyr yarsu"caraf nazeerat tacabe wlhy mommy azubarda cikin kawai,yaushe zaki zauna kisawa kanki damuwa,aidaukarta kawaizakiyi kikai awanke cikin kowa yahuta kinga iyayen nata bama zasusan taje tayi wani cikin shegeba"rinsa ido nayi inajin wani irin kuna araina,ahankali nakusa kaina parlour tunkan nakaraso hankalin jama ardake ciki kafyadawo kaina,sainaji kamar inama kasatasage   nashige ciki, na isa dakyar nazauna  kasa kusada kafafunta,ahankali nace gani hajja  umma"harkuma lokacin batayi shiru damaganarba"tacigaba,waima haryanzu batafadi wanda  yymata cikinba.Rukayya dake zaune gifenta tace to kintabajin mecikin shege yafadi wanda  yymasa dawuri aisai anhadamasa daduka tukun zaifada"anty surayya takalli  mommy tace yanzu daman tuntuninna batafadi Wanda yymata cikinbane?yanzu mommy shine kkzubamata ido baki tisiyeta saita fadamikiba"aibayan antisiyeta tafada akaramata da duka sanna aje azubar dacikin"wata wacce yau nafara ganinta itama  tace ai irinsu dama maganin irinsu saihaka,akwai  wata ma aikaciyar asibiti ana kaimata irinsu masuyin cikin shenna agida take zubarmusu"kawai gidan za akaita tazubardashi"tunda sukafara maganar hawaye kebin fuskata idan mukahada idoda anty Asma'u saita girgizamun kai, hajja umma tace ya isahaka maganar.takalleni tace yarna wanene ya aikatamiki wanna mummunar aikin? shiru nayi saihawayenda ketayimin zarya afuska"nazeerat tace dan   sabarrashin mutunci anayiki magana kinajin mutane bazaki fadi  wanda yy miki cikinba , matarna itama tadakamin sawa,bazaki fadaba"nanma shuru nadadayi" tace Hajiya ba fa zatafada tadadiba"yanzudai akaita aje awanke cikin inyaso sauran ayi daga baya"nazeerat da Rukayya sukace hakan za ayi" mommy tanisa tace"kai zubarda cikifa kamar kasherai yake"ni inagani abar zubarda cikinna...sukayi saurincewa"mommy zubarda cikinnafa shine rufin asirin gidanna,dan  wlhy duk kwatancen daza ayi dole sai ansa wanna dagidanna akan wanna shigen cikin,kawai azubardashi.....WLHY DUK'WANDA YAKUSKURA YASAKE SHEGANTA ABINDA KECIKINTA KOKUMA KUKAYI YUNKURIN ZUBARMIN DA CIKI WLHY SAINA DAURE MUTUM DAURINDA KODUNIYARNA KAFDANGINSANE BAZASUTABA IYA KWANCESABA!!!!!yymaganar cikin sananin fusata hadeda firgida duk maisauraro................



Kuyi maneji hakori yasanigaba

馃吙43馃憠馃徎44




""""""" kaf ilahirin jama'ar dakegun bbwanda bai firgita da irin tsawar dayadakaba,nikaina saida hantarcikina yakada kaf mukajuyo mukalalli inda maganar yafito,saukowa yake daga matattakalar bine cikin zafinnama yake sauka haryana hada step,ganin maimaganar yasani mutuwar zaune. kaibani kadaiba hattasu saida suka firgita daganin  daga garesa maganar tafito "yafado parlour yana huci tareda nunasu da danyasa gabaki dayansu yakebinsu damugun kallo fuskarsa yarikide yakoma tamkar nazaki sai huci yake yanabin kowannesu dawani irin kallo yana kada yasarsa alamar gargadi"saikuma yagirgiza kai yajuya dasauri kamar  zaitashisama yabar parlour din yaje yashiga motarsa yaja yabar gidan...tunda yafara maganar mommy tabude  baki tana binsa dakallon mamaki,saiyanzu dayafita tajuyo dakallonta  gareni"sitt palon yy kamar andauke ruwansama" saiwanna yakalli wanna wanna yakalli wanna"hajja umma ce  tayikarfin halincewa IBRAHIMA,waikam kokunji abinda wanna dan kefada kuwa?waifa adaina sheganta masa ciki"wani irin kururuwa nazeerat tayi,tatuma salle  saigata asakiyar parlour tamulmulo wani babban ashar takunduma, tayi kaina tanafadin niza aci amanata towallahi saina kasheki nakashe abinda yakecikinnaki"dasauri hajja umma tatareta tace ke nazeeratu kinada hankalikuwa"tace da alla sakeni niza ashiryawa manakisa,yar iska tacacciyar karuwa, to wlh ba ayi macenda zan hada miji da itaba"nakasheki nakashe banza yarmasiyata"takuma yinkaina yanzukam mommy ce tadakatar da ita tahanyar dakamata tsawa" amma kosauraran ta batayiba,tacigaba dafadin sainakasheki wlh bazan barkiba tunda har karuwancinki tasallake kan yayan talakawa yadawo kan mijina, tadunfaroni gadan gadan"anty Asma'u tayi saurin shigewa sakaninmu,ummee tazo tajanye hannuna takaini daki tace insa key taciki.aiko dasauri namurza key din"inajin ihu da hargowarda nazeerat take"duk kuwa wanda yymata magana saita gayamasa mummunar magana"tadau mayafinta tafice fuuu kamar sabon kamu,nan parlour yyshiru kowa dakalar abinda kesakawa aransa" bangaren Rukayya kuwa zuciyarta tafarfasa take wani irin sanan RUMAINA yadada baibayeta,lallai dasakel tafada tareda mikewa saye tashige daki...hajja umma takalle mommy tace waimeke faruwane kam menene hadin IBRAHIM da wanna yar daharzai danganta kansa da dancikinta"mommy tasauke numfashi tace wlh hajja bansan komai gameda wanna lamarinba"hajja umma tace ja irin yaro zaidawo yasameni  muzaikawowa iyashege"harda yiwamutane jan ido danuna shaferinsu na sojoji"mumunzo mun titsiye yarinya tafadi wanda yymata ciki "ashe shine kinibebbe,to wlh zaizo yasameni"mommy dai kala bataceba.tulin mmk ne  yahanata iyacewa komai....
Zubewa nayi sakiyar dakin sakamakon jinwani irin juyi dakaina yakemin" sunan Allah nashiga anbata,harnadan farajin saukin abinda nakejidin"waishin nekam kodai akwai laifinda nayiwa ubangiji ne yake hukuntani da irin wanna hukuncin"saikuma nayisaurin yin istigifari "me ya***I'B kenufi daharzaice kada a zubarmasa daciki" menene dalilinsa nadanganta cikinna dashi meyasa meyasa yasubhanallah waishinkan mekefaruwa daninekam"agun nazame nakwanta nacikukana ma ishi harbarcin wahala tadaukeni...
Koda 
nazeerat  tafita motarta tashiga taje gida kodaidaita parking batayiba tafito tanufi cikin gidan,direct dakinsa tanufa,tanashiga taga baya dakin tashige har bathroom nanma bayanan,tafito tarika wurgi dakayakin cikin parlour,tana fadin wlh ***I'B baka  isaba yau inna saidai ayiduk abinda za ayi" ni inanan sainayi dagaske kafin kakusanceni"ashedama ka aje watace  agefe harda  yimata ciki nikuma inanan kobatar wata bantabayiba" haka tarika hauka hartagaji dankanta tazube saman kujera.....
Bani nafarkaba saidaf magrib nayi mmkn yadda nayi barci mainisa haka,nalallaba nashiga bathroom nayi wanka tareda dauro alaula  nafito"bayan na idar dasallah ina zaune bisakan sallayar.naji ana knocking nannaji soro yakamani"saida naji muryar ummee tanafadin bad'd'o nice,namike na isa jikin kofar sanda tadada cewa kibude mana,najidai zahirin itace kafin nabude "tana shiga namaida kofar narufe,ta isa ta aje plate inda ke hannuta" tadubeni tace zauna kici abinci,nace nakoshi.tace mekkci?"nayi shuru "tace  zauna kici natabbata yau tunsafe bakisa komai acikinkiba" ummee banajin yunwa,tace kitura haka.har idan kkbi narashin jinyunwanna zai illatar dake .duk wanda yakecikin  hali irinnakinna bazaitaba jinyunwaba.amma rashincin abincin zai iyaxamemasa illa.amma idan yadaure yacidin zaitaimaka masa kotahanyar jinkarfin jikinsa. kinji"kai nagyada mata, najanyo plate in narika sakurar abincin.nakuwa ci kusanrabi"namike nashiga bathroom nawanke bakina nafito nazauna"kusada ummee"ummee tadubeni nimadai itanake kallon dan naga tanbayoyi dauke afuskarta,tace bad'd'o"nayisaurin cewa ummee bansan komaiba wlh abinda ya***I'B yafada bagaskiyabace danni koda maganar baki bata taba hadani dashiba  ummee kogaisuwata baya amsawa,nimakuma nadaina gaidashin"nidai kawai nasan yafadi hakanne dansaboda tsanata dayayi" ido ummee takuramin harnakai karshen maganata,sanna taja numfashi tasauke,tace amma lallai RUMAINA keyarinyace haryanzu, kinsan waye ***I'B nakowa kuwa?" Kidaina tunanin abinda yafada karyace dan  shiba  karamin mutun bane akan meye zaibata lokacinsa wajen fadar karya akanki" mekk taremasa" kinsan dubbannin darurruwan manyan mutanen dayake huldadasukuwa,tokidaina tunanin hakan watakilama baisan kinananba harsailokacinda bukatarsa tasanar masa"kallonta nayi dannagaza fahimtar abinda take nufu"nace kamarya harsai lokacinda bukatarsa tasanarmasa" tayi murmushi tareda gyara zamanta tace" RUMAINA  Allah yymiki baiwar halittarda babu wani namijinda zaiganki baiji wani abu aransaba"hatta mace yar uwarki idan takalleki saita kuma,  RUMAINA ya***I'B zai iyayen komai idan yaso tahanyarda bazaki taba saniba"tunda yafurta dabakinsa to yatabbata ciki nasane" kuka nafashe dashi,nace amma Allah ya'isa sakanina dashi.yacuceni yacuci  rayuwata"yarukuzamin farincikina yalalatamin burina,yanzun nadawo rageggiya agurin mijinda zan aura,nayi burin kasancewa acikin yanmata masukai budurcinsu gidan mijinsu"ummee kullum nasihata da mama baiwuce  nasare kaina budurcina shine yancina agidan  aurenaba"wlh koda wani baizubar da cikinanba nisaina zubardashi "tace abin akwai ciwo amma hakuri shine magani,kada kikasherai danshi baidauki hakkin kowaba,kosauraranta banayi nasha alwashin saina zubarda cikinna " datagadai basauraranta zanyiba saitatafi"daren ranar nisa yamin"saigani nake kamar gari bazaiwayeba"dakyar barci yadaukeni kiransallar farko akunnena"naje nayi alaula nayi nafila inakan sallaya " har akashiga masallaci...karfe takwas daidai nafito daga wanka"nashirya saf,inayi inaduban agogo, nabata minti talatin wajen shiryawa,inagamawa nabude  wardrobe naciro kudi wanda my nass  yabani tunda dadewa na aje agun,nasa shi cikin karamar jakar hannu" nakoma nazauna bakin gado,idona naka agogo" lokacin yaki gudu,inanan zaune agogon yabuga karfe 10 zunbur namike  saye nadau hijjab nasaka,na isa nabude kofa nafita"harna  isa part insu ummee banhaduda kowaba,bedroom inta nashiga nataddata tana breakfast.tana ganina tamike saye,nace ummee  muje kirakani.tawaro ido tace ina?nace asibiti,.tace RUMAINA kifajanne batun zubarda cikinna dan wlh...nayi saurin dakatar da ita tahanyar dagamata hannu nace ya isa indai bazaki rakaniba shikena.najuya nafita dasauri...........

馃吙45馃憠馃徎46




"""""" Tabiyoni dasauri tanafadin RUMAINA kadafa kiyi yunkurin aikata abinda kkson aikata wanna"kinjifa abinda yafada jiya,akan dukwanda yy yunkurin zubarmasa daciki,shine kedakanki zaki aikata hakan" kosauraranta banyiba nayi gaba abina.inafitowa,nahangi driver yana goge motoci"na isa nagaidashi"nace mlm sule unguwa zakane?,yace a'a ba inda zani kawaidai inagogesune saboda kodamasu bukatar fita yanzu,nace yauwa tomuje kakaini unguwa,yacetoh,yabude marfin motar, nashiga,shima yazaga yashiga, muna zuwa Gert  infarko yy Horn madadin Gert tabude saiganin wani katon soja yadunfaromu" yana zuwa yace ya sule inazuwa haka" mln sule yace unguwa zankaita" sojan yace cikin hausarsa dabata zaunaba,yau munada doka  bafita akoma,akoma,yabuga jikin motar yana daga hannu alamar koma,ganindai zahiri babari zaiyi mufitanba,natattaro jarumtata nayi karfin halin cewa.mommy ce ta aikemu"yace No bafita akoma"mln sule yajuya zaikoma,araina nace katon banza abinda ka iyafada kena akoma akoma"hausarma kodadi batayimasaba"sai kuma sojan yajuyo,yysaurin zuwa jikin motar yaleko ni yace kince hajiya,kainagyda masa dasauri"saiyabuga jikin motar,OK kuje kuje,yafada yana daga mana hannu...munafita mlm sule yace inazamune? Shiuro nayi inatunanin wacce asibiti zanje wanda yanzu munazuwa za acire min cikin sainayi tunanin komai akace babba to babbanne danhaka  nayanke hukunci gara naje babban asibiti"sainace masa, teaching hospital,yace to, yajuya akalar tafiyar izuwa T.H hospital, muna isa naceda mln sule yajirani yanzu  zandawo"yaceto ,bin asibitin nayi dakallo, danganin girmansa kokarshensa bana gani"nazari nafarayi dan  narasa ta inazanfara"sainafarabin komai akarance inayi  inalurada jama'a yanda sukeyi ahaka harnakammala komai inazaune alayi duk nagaji kunsan yanayin babban asibiti bakamar karaba bace dole saikasha wanna wahalar" nazauna baifi da 10min ba naji anfara kiran sunana,nayi hamdala tareda mikewa saye,jama'ar dakegun sukafara mita sunafadin yaza ayi yanxu nazo kuma ace har file ina ina yashiga offece in Dr"nidai gaba nayi abina,nashiga offece  in dasallama,Dr ya amsa tareda nunamin gurin zama"nazauna batareda nace komaiba"ganin nayishiru yasashi dagowa yakalleni, saiyace meke damunki"nasunkuyar dakaina kasa nantake naji hawaye yacika  min ido"yakumace kenake sauraro"baki narawa nace" um..um..um..dama dama.nakuma yinshiru,namarasa ta ina zanfara"ya***I'B kacuceni yanzu taya zansanarwa likitanna abinda ketafe dani"nasan kallon yar iska zaiyimin,nafada  araina. saikawai nafashe dakuka, barin rubutun dayake yy yasaya yana kallona,saikuma ya jinjina kai,yace ya isa mekikeso amiki?"cikin kukan nace sone aciremin ciki.yace OK badamuwa, yakalli wata datake zaune daga cangefe yace,maryam kuje ayimata aiki"tace OK sir,tamike tace dani zomuje ko"da dan  mmk nakallesu dan  banyi zaton haka dawuriba,namike asanyaye muka fita da  ita,tafiya maidannisa mukayi,kafin muka isa kofar wani offece tasanya makulli tabude  tashiga niko sayuwa nayi tajuyo tace shigo mana,nashiga tace hauna kafinna  kicire hijjab inki, tanunamin Dan madaidaicin gado,nacire hajjab ina sanna nahaura gadon,nan tashiga jona na urori,tana gamawa tace to barinayimiki  scanning dannaga ta inazamu fara,nace to asanyaye,nantafara yimin scanning,idanta  akan "computer tace kash menake gani haka,saitakashe na uwar,tace tace tashi kizauna,namike nazauna,itama tazauna bakin gadon,tace bincikenda nayi yanzu,bazai yuwu acire cikinba,saboda akwai masala,har idan kuwa akace za aciren tokuwa za ayi biyu babu,inanufin zaki iya  rasa ranki" kuma duk inda  kkje sukacemiki zasu iyaciremiki tokuwa inamai tabbatar miki,rankice sukenufi zaibar jikinki"sai tamike saye tace amma idan kinada ja zaki Iya zuwa wani asibitin"takashe na urorin"asanyaye namike saye.soro duk yagama rufeni.nadau hijjab ina  nasaka nafita batareda naceda ita kalaba...........
